Mopatis_1 = { 
	name = Illyrio # Canon, THE Illyrio Mopatis
	dynasty = dynn_Mopatis
	dna = Mopatis_1

	martial = 3
	diplomacy = 6
	intrigue = 10
	stewardship = 6
	learning = 3
	prowess = 5
 
	religion = rhllor
	culture = pentoshi

	trait = education_stewardship_4
	trait = physique_good_1
	trait = greedy
	trait = ambitious
	trait = gregarious
	trait = charming

	disallow_random_traits = yes

	8255.1.1 = { 
		birth = yes 
		add_character_flag = canon_status_canon
	}
	8271.1.1 = { 
		effect = { add_trait = education_martial_prowess_2 }
	}
	8275.1.1 = { add_spouse = Narratys_57 } # Nerria Narratys, cousin to Prince of Pentos
	8279.1.1 = {
		effect = { remove_trait = education_martial_prowess_2 }
		trait = education_republican_knowledge_4
		trait = gluttonous
		trait = fashionable
	}
	8281.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = Mopatis_hh_1 # Serra
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { character:Narratys_1 = { is_alive = yes } }
				reverse_add_opinion = {
					target = character:Narratys_1 # Yoro Narratys
					modifier = insulted_opinion
				}
			}		
		}
	}
}
### Household
Mopatis_hh_1 = {
	name = Serra # Canon, married Illyrio Mopatis
	female = yes
 
	religion = rhllor
	culture = lyseni

	trait = beauty_good_2
	
	8258.1.1 = { 
		birth = yes 
		add_character_flag = canon_status_canon
		if = { # Remove is Saera Jayn is alive
			limit = { game_start_date < 8258.12.21 }
			death = { death_reason = death_vanished }
		}
	}
	8278.1.1 = { employer = Mopatis_1 } # Illyrio Mopatis
	8284.1.1 = {
		trait = greyscale
		death = { death_reason = death_greyscale }
	}
}
